INC-SOURCE (PHOTO) Neutrons produced by (g,n) and (g,f)           2296500100025 
            reactions induced via Bremsstrahlung from the         2296500100026

DETECTOR   (IOCH) The alpha-particles were detected using a       2296500100035 
            Frisch-gridded ionization chamber filled with         2296500100036 
            ultra pure C-H4 as detector gas.                      2296500100037 
           (BF3) BF3 proportional counters were located at        2296500100038 
            different places above the neutron source. Their      2296500100039 
            output is used to normalize spectra to the same total 2296500100040 
            neutron flux.                                         2296500100041 
MONITOR    (5-B-10(N,A)3-LI-7,,SIG) The neutron flux is           2296500100042 
            determined based on the well-known reaction using     2296500100043 
            a B-10 sample in an ionization chamber. The data      2296500100044 
            from ENDF/B-VI are used.                              2296500100045 
SAMPLE     .Evaporated elemental boron (7.17+-0.13)E+19 atoms     2296500100046 
CORRECTION .Background corrections for flux and capture:          2296500100047 
            * based on Au, Co, Mn, Rh and W black resonances      2296500100048 
            * deduced from a fit - using AGS - of the background  2296500100049 
              points with a function like: BG(TOF)=a*TOF**b+c,    2296500100050 
              with a,b and c adjustable parameters and TOF        2296500100051 
              the neutron time-of-flight.                         2296500100052 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-T) total uncertainties were deduced by propagating2296500100053
